# Project Status Board (Source of Truth)

**Status:** ACTIVE  
**Last Updated (UTC):** 2026-04-03
**Owner:** Engineering  
**Scope:** Live delivery status for features, quality gates, and release readiness.

---

## Rules of Use

1. This file is the only live status source of truth.
2. Any status change must include fresh evidence in this file (tests, workflow run, or commit/PR).
3. Update this board in the same PR/commit as the implementation change whenever possible.
4. If no status changed, add a short timestamped "No Change" entry in `Status Change Log`.
5. Keep detailed implementation narratives in `docs/plans/*`; keep this board concise and evidence-linked.

---

## Consolidated Source Inputs

This board consolidates progress from:

- `docs/plans/2026-02-26-full-rebuild.md` (target scope roadmap)

| Word list + ePub import | DONE | Review-first generic word lists with cached source imports and mixed word/phrase entries | Branch-local implementation now includes migration-backed runtime proof on an isolated branch DB, focused browser proof on an isolated frontend+Playwright stack, full backend/frontend suite coverage, explicit concurrent exact-source proof with two live Celery workers on the `imports` queue, and PR hardening for the final review/CI pass. The branch proved `upload -> worker processing -> review entries -> create list -> fetch list` against a real PostgreSQL schema after migration `044`; fixed the async `MissingGreenlet` issue in create-list by loading `ImportSource` explicitly from `job.import_source_id`; fixed a second fresh-import `MissingGreenlet` on the cache-miss path by caching `user_id` before the `get_or_create_import_source()` commit boundary; and hardened source processing with a per-source Postgres advisory lock so duplicate worker deliveries serialize on the canonical `ImportSource`. The learner UX now separates the two related features cleanly: `/imports` handles upload/review/create, `/word-lists` owns ongoing list management, the homepage exposes distinct learner entry cards for each, and `/imports` reloads recent jobs from `GET /api/import-jobs` instead of losing terminal rows on refresh. The branch Docker stack also supports shared lexicon artifacts through `WORDS_DATA_DIR`, which was verified by recreating the branch containers with the main repo `data/` directory mounted into `/app/data`. The browser proof covers `upload -> processing -> review -> create list -> open list -> rename list -> manual add -> remove item -> re-add quoted phrase`, and the live concurrent proof shows two fresh uploads landing on the same `import_source_id` with exactly one `source_import_extraction_started` log and one `source_import_reused_completed_cache` log across two workers. The PR hardening pass removed the list-read full-matcher rebuild, preserved descriptions on rename-only PATCH, fixed multi-row CSV bulk parsing, converted invalid import-job selections into `400` responses, and taught the aggregate E2E gate to treat skipped admin/user jobs as neutral rather than failed. Compatibility routes remain in place, but there is no obvious remaining product or concurrency gap on this slice. | `backend/app/models/import_source.py`, `backend/app/models/import_source_entry.py`, `backend/app/models/word_list_item.py`, `backend/alembic/versions/044_add_import_sources_and_generic_word_list_items.py`, `backend/app/services/source_imports.py`, `backend/app/api/word_lists.py`, `backend/app/api/import_jobs.py`, `backend/app/tasks/epub_processing.py`, `frontend/src/app/imports/page.tsx`, `frontend/src/app/word-lists/page.tsx`, `frontend/src/components/word-lists-manager.tsx`, `frontend/src/app/page.tsx`, `frontend/src/app/imports/__tests__/page.test.tsx`, `frontend/src/lib/imports-client.ts`, `backend/tests/test_source_imports_service.py`, `backend/tests/test_imports_api.py`, `backend/tests/test_import_jobs_api.py`, `backend/tests/test_word_lists_api.py`, `backend/tests/test_epub_processing.py`, `e2e/tests/full/user-import-review-create.full.spec.ts`, `e2e/tests/full/user-import-terminal.full.spec.ts`, `scripts/verify_epub_import_concurrency.py`, `docker-compose.yml`, `docker-compose.browser-proof.yml`, `.github/workflows/ci.yml` | Rerun PR #103 CI and merge once green |
| Review + SM-2 queue | DONE (non-voice) | Queue add/due/submit/stats + full integration | The learner review flow now exposes entry-level semantics end-to-end: `/review` follows challenge -> relearn or reveal -> schedule, `/reviews` returns richer prompt/detail/schedule payloads, and the scheduler uses an adaptive outcome/prompt-type interval model instead of plain SM-2. Runtime scheduling prefers dedicated `entry_review_states` and falls back to the legacy queue/history layer only for compatibility; failed reviews persist explicit relearning/recheck state; prompt generation now includes `meaning_discrimination`, `collocation_check`, `situation_matching`, `typed_recall`, and a non-live `speak_recall` placeholder path; entry-review events capture prompt-family, parent-entry, target-type, response-input, replay-count, and scheduling analytics fields; and `/api/reviews/analytics/summary` now exposes recent prompt-family/outcome/input-mode counts plus audio replay totals for operational reporting. Follow-up review fixes are now in place: `definition_to_entry` grades against the entry text, `entry_to_definition` / `audio_to_definition` grade against the definition text, phrase learning cards submit against the backing `EntryReviewState` instead of dropping answers when `queue_item_id` was null, weak distractor pools now collapse to real 3-choice MCQs instead of padded filler, and word-form prompts prefer `word_confusables` before generic fallback distractors. The review settings slice now adds durable review-depth presets plus confidence/word/audio spelling and picture toggles, and the review card builder honors those preferences when selecting prompts and scheduling the next review. The security/performance hardening pass is also in place: client-visible answer truth has been removed, prompt tokens are now opaque encrypted blobs instead of readable JWT payloads, objective grading is server-authoritative, duplicate queue submits are idempotent per prompt, due-state reads lock the row before mutation, due queues overfetch before sibling-bury trimming, distractor selection avoids `ORDER BY random()` hot-path scans, grading no longer depends on client-reported timing, objective submits now ignore forged client `remember`/`lookup` outcomes and resolve semantics from the issued prompt token, and same-day distractor pools are reused per request to cut repeated due-queue query load. The latest architecture follow-up now also makes `/api/reviews/queue/due` hydrate only the current card while fetching later cards on demand via `GET /api/reviews/queue/{id}`, which cut average due-request query count roughly in half or better on the isolated benchmark and lifted throughput materially across every measured stage without breaking the learner review flow. A dedicated isolated-stack benchmark now exists for the review path, and the current dev-stack baseline stays error-free through `50` concurrent benchmark users while still meeting the initial `p95 < 500ms` bar through `5` VUs on a single local Docker host; that is a stronger baseline than before, but still not a production concurrency claim. | `backend/app/api/reviews.py`, `backend/app/services/review.py`, `backend/app/services/review_submission.py`, `backend/app/spaced_repetition.py`, `backend/app/models/entry_review.py`, `backend/alembic/versions/028_add_entry_review_tables.py`, `backend/alembic/versions/029_add_entry_review_event_analytics_fields.py`, `backend/alembic/versions/041_add_due_queue_indexes_to_entry_review_states.py`, `backend/alembic/versions/042_add_last_submission_prompt_id_to_entry_review_states.py`, `backend/tests/test_review_service.py`, `backend/tests/test_review_api.py`, `frontend/src/app/review/page.tsx`, `frontend/src/app/review/__tests__/page.test.tsx`, `frontend/src/lib/knowledge-map-client.ts`, `benchmarks/k6/review-dev.js`, `scripts/benchmark/run-review-dev-benchmark.sh`, `docs/reports/2026-04-02-review-dev-capacity-report.md`, `e2e/tests/smoke/user-review-submit.smoke.spec.ts`, `e2e/tests/smoke/user-review-prompt-families.smoke.spec.ts`, `e2e/tests/smoke/user-review-typed-normalization.smoke.spec.ts`, `docs/plans/2026-03-27-entry-review-system-implementation.md`, `docs/plans/2026-04-02-review-scale-hardening-plan.md` | Replace the speech placeholder with real voice capture/playback once audio input is available |
| E2E + CI quality gates | DONE | Required smoke-first PR gate aligned with Docker runtime | CI now reports `E2E Smoke (required)` first and only starts `E2E Full (required)` after smoke passes, so PRs fail fast without dropping the full-suite gate. The Docker runtime and E2E DB helper share the same Postgres credential, Playwright remains serialized to eliminate container-contention flakes, and the fresh local proof set is clean across targeted backend/frontend review regressions plus Docker-based smoke and full Playwright runs. The isolated review stack now also proves the current branch migrates from empty DB through revision `042`, then passes the hardened review browser smoke suite against branch-local backend/frontend containers rather than the shared dev stack. CI now also makes learner review/SRS coverage explicit instead of only implicit: the backend and frontend jobs each run a named review/SRS regression subset, and a dedicated `E2E Review + SRS Smoke (required)` gate runs the stable learner review-core Playwright slice before the broader smoke lane. The real file-backed voice playback smoke remains valuable evidence, but it is no longer part of the required `@smoke` gate because it is more environment-sensitive than the core review flow. | `.github/workflows/ci.yml`, `frontend/package.json`, `e2e/package.json`, `e2e/playwright.config.ts`, `e2e/tests/helpers/auth.ts`, `e2e/tests/smoke/user-review-submit.smoke.spec.ts`, `e2e/tests/smoke/user-review-prompt-families.smoke.spec.ts`, `e2e/tests/smoke/user-review-typed-normalization.smoke.spec.ts`, `e2e/tests/smoke/user-learner-audio.smoke.spec.ts`, `e2e/tests/smoke/user-real-voice-playback.smoke.spec.ts`, `backend/tests/test_review_service.py`, `frontend/src/app/review/__tests__/page.test.tsx`, `admin-frontend/src/app/lexicon/import-db/page.tsx`, `docker-compose.review-isolated.yml`, `backend/alembic/versions/042_add_last_submission_prompt_id_to_entry_review_states.py` | Maintain gate health and widen coverage only when the stack can support it deterministically |

| Concept learning (synsets, R/U/L) | PARTIAL | Phase 4 concepts/mastery system | The learner-facing knowledge-map slice now spans a fuller learner shell: `/` is a screenshot-aligned mobile dashboard, `/knowledge-map` is now the full-board overview only, `/knowledge-map/range/[start]` owns the detailed cards/tags/list view for a specific 100-entry bucket, `/knowledge-list/[status]` exposes filtered sortable learner lists, `/search` is now a standalone learner search tab with recent history and direct entry jump, `/word/[entryId]` and `/phrase/[entryId]` are the only learner detail routes, and `/settings` exposes learner preferences. The backend now hydrates learner list/search/range/detail cards from a normalized phrase learner schema rather than serving phrase learner text from `compiled_payload`; phrase senses now persist locale-aware definitions/example translations plus per-sense learner metadata, and the importer replaces normalized phrase children on re-import. Persisted user preferences also include a global `show_translations_by_default` flag. The frontend now renders English and localized translation consistently in the range list cards and standalone detail views, normalizes placeholder translation strings away, and memoizes the hottest translation-derivation paths in both range-detail and detail overlay flows. Review/SM-2 remains meaning-level and is not yet linked back into entry-status progression, example-level translations are still unavailable in the word schema, and learner image assets are still placeholders because the current schema has no real image field. | `backend/app/api/knowledge_map.py`, `backend/app/api/user_preferences.py`, `backend/app/services/knowledge_map.py`, `backend/app/models/learner_entry_status.py`, `backend/app/models/user_preference.py`, `backend/app/models/search_history.py`, `backend/app/models/phrase_sense.py`, `backend/app/models/phrase_sense_localization.py`, `backend/app/models/phrase_sense_example.py`, `backend/app/models/phrase_sense_example_localization.py`, `backend/alembic/versions/016_add_learner_knowledge_map_tables.py`, `backend/alembic/versions/017_add_user_preference_translation_visibility.py`, `backend/alembic/versions/019_normalize_phrase_learner_fields.py`, `tools/lexicon/import_db.py`, `frontend/src/app/page.tsx`, `frontend/src/app/knowledge-map/page.tsx`, `frontend/src/app/knowledge-map/range/[start]/page.tsx`, `frontend/src/app/knowledge-list/[status]/page.tsx`, `frontend/src/app/search/page.tsx`, `frontend/src/app/word/[entryId]/page.tsx`, `frontend/src/app/phrase/[entryId]/page.tsx`, `frontend/src/app/settings/page.tsx`, `frontend/src/components/knowledge-map-range-detail.tsx`, `frontend/src/components/knowledge-entry-detail-page.tsx`, `frontend/src/components/learner-shell-nav.tsx`, `frontend/src/lib/knowledge-map-client.ts`, `frontend/src/lib/user-preferences-client.ts`, `frontend/src/lib/auth-route-guard.ts`, `frontend/src/middleware.ts` | Connect entry statuses to review/stats flows, add real learner image/example-translation assets if the word schema grows to support them, and replace the remaining screenshot-only placeholder settings with real product behavior |
| Lexicon admin enrichment rollout | PARTIAL | Learner-first offline lexicon builder produces staged common-word entries plus learner-facing enrichment for local DB import | The words slice now supports shared entry metadata (`entry_id`, `entry_type`, `normalized_form`, `source_provenance`), a `wordfreq` top-words inventory path via `build-base --top-words` / `--rollout-stage`, deterministic pre-build canonicalization that collapses only morphology-backed variants into canonical headwords while keeping semantic neighbors separate and preserving learner-worthy related forms as linked standalone entries, snapshot-side registry/status artifacts plus `lookup-entry` / `status-entry` operator commands, learner-translation generation for `zh-Hans`, `es`, `ar`, `pt-BR`, and `ja`, an optional bounded ambiguous-form adjudication path via `detect-ambiguous-forms`, `adjudicate-forms`, and `build-base --adjudications`, direct per-word enrichment writes to `words.enriched.jsonl` plus checkpoint/decision/failure sidecars for resumable 1K -> 5K -> 30K runs, and a safer ambiguous-tail operator gate that defers unresolved variant-form tails from base outputs until adjudication while exposing pending state in lookup/status and validation. The phrase slice now has reviewed-CSV phrase inventory ingestion, a bounded `senses[]` phrase enrichment schema, realtime phrase enrichment into compiled artifacts, phrase-aware compile/review/import persistence, and admin review panels that surface structured phrase details instead of leaving phrase payloads only in raw JSON. Realtime enrichment now uses lower configurable retry budgets via `--transient-retries` and `--validation-retries`, phrase translation `usage_note` validation is conditional on whether the source phrase note exists, operators get shared lexicon CLI runtime logging via `--log-level` / `--log-file` across the broader tool surface with per-command progress plus per-lexeme retry/failure tracing in `enrich`, and the active toolchain no longer exposes legacy `per_sense` mode or treats `enrichments.jsonl` as a supported realtime artifact path. Successful per-word realtime completions now append immediately to `words.enriched.jsonl`, `enrich.checkpoint.jsonl`, and `enrich.decisions.jsonl` even after earlier failures, while `enrich.failures.jsonl` is preserved as append-only failure history across resumes and checkpoint remains the only skip ledger for completed lexemes. The batch lexicon slice is now wired through submit/status/ingest/retry/QC commands over JSONL ledgers, with deterministic request/result lineage, append-only ingest for accepted rows, a separate failure sidecar, retry attempt bumping, and review-queue generation for failed rows. The admin tool is now structured around the current compiled-artifact workflow instead of the older staged-selection flow: `/lexicon/ops` serves as the snapshot-first hub, `/lexicon/compiled-review` remains the DB-backed review staging path, `/lexicon/jsonl-review` remains the file-backed path, `/lexicon/import-db` exposes dry-run and explicit final DB import for approved compiled artifacts, `/lexicon/db-inspector` gives post-import verification against the live DB, and the old selection-review page has been demoted to `/lexicon/legacy`. A separate compiled-review admin tool now sits between compiled JSONL export and DB import: admins can import immutable compiled artifacts, inspect item-level validator/QC metadata in `/lexicon/compiled-review`, persist approve/reject/reopen decisions plus regeneration requests in dedicated `lexicon_artifact_review_*` tables, export canonical decision overlays for `review-materialize`, and export approved/rejected/regenerate JSONL directly from the backend, with Playwright smoke now covering compiled review, JSONL review, and the new Ops -> Import DB -> DB Inspector loop. The 30K rollout path now uses tracked irregular-form datasets for audited noun/plural, compound irregular plural, and irregular verb misses; curated surface-form drops for bounded inventory noise like `childrens`, `womens`, `dont`, `atleast`, `bl`, `seperate`, `longterm`, and `lyin`; anomaly rows for lexicalized plural false positives such as `clothes`, `goods`, `spirits`, `arms`, `quarters`, and `regards`; explicit entity-category data for non-general rows (`name`, `place`, `brand`, `entity_other`); bounded tail exclusions for concrete bad admissions without widening canonical heuristics; and distinct-derived variant metadata for words like `building`, `charming`, and `ceiling`, driven by tracked data first with bounded inference fallback. The current per-word enrichment prompt is now both entity-category-aware and distinct-variant-aware, and has been further hardened to compress high-frequency function-word sense sprawl while preserving important closed-class grammar words and preferring base-word linkage for kept inflected special cases. The current exact deterministic 30K snapshot is `data/lexicon/snapshots/words-30000-20260314-main-real-entity-tail-hardened` with `requested_top_words=39485`, `30000` lexemes, `63126` senses, `56507` concepts, `0` unresolved ambiguous rows, `0` snapshot validation errors, and audit-side explicit entity counts `name=36`, `place=11`, `brand=5`, `entity_other=4`. Lexicon-owned persisted data now lives in the dedicated Postgres `lexicon` schema while runtime/app tables stay separate in the same database; translated example/usage-note fields remain artifact-only in this slice. The structured-output schema for the enrichment path has now been hardened to the gateway's strict requirements, and a completed fixed-schema `curated_100` live matrix shows `word_only` clearly outperforming `grounded` operationally. `gpt-5-nano word_only` remains the recommended 30K default (`399` valid rows, `0` failed lexemes, `4` repairs, `21.965s` average latency), with `gpt-5.1 word_only` as the conservative fallback (`398` valid rows, `0` failed lexemes, `3` repairs, `23.816s` average latency). A follow-up grouped-request benchmark on `curated_16` was then used to test batched enrichment and was rejected as a rollout path: `g4` and `g8` runs failed badly under 60-second transport timeouts, and the only non-failing grouped case with plausible speed (`gpt-5.1 g2`) was too small and fragile to justify the extra operational complexity or larger failure blast radius. The rollout contract has now been switched to the approved `wordfreq + LLM` direction for the 30K path: `build-base --top-words` snapshots are truly WordNet-free, `word_only` enrichment now validates a word-level decision schema (`discard`, `keep_standard`, `keep_derived_special`) instead of LLM-selected `sense_id` rows, compile/export synthesizes internal meaning IDs after validation so DB import compatibility stays intact, and the tail-exclusion dataset now drops out-of-scope admissions such as `a`, `an`, and single-letter alphabet rows before enrichment. The final bounded live pilot at `data/lexicon/snapshots/words-100-20260316-wordfreq-only-live-pilot-v4-final/snapshot` finished with `93` completed lexemes, `93` explicit decision rows, `368` enrichment rows, `89` compiled words, and `0` failures; compared with the earlier `v2` pilot, compiled sense density dropped from mean `5.295` / median `7` / max `8` to mean `4.135` / median `5` / max `5` while preserving the intended boundary behavior for tested edge cases (`is/are/has` discard, `their/its/our` keep, `said` derived-special in focused recheck). The tool is now operationally ready for the resumable 30K run, with the main residual risk shifted from durability to normal live-model semantic variance on borderline form-family words such as ## Current Top Gaps (Priority Order)

1. Implement dictionary API fallback for `/api/words/lookup` misses + tests.
2. Move import source storage from local/container temp paths to object storage (or equivalent shared ephemeral layer) with guaranteed cleanup on completion/failure and periodic TTL cleanup.
3. Beta-release activation: wire real deploy/promote variables and pass full tagged promotion drill.
4. Concept learning (synsets, R/U/L) phase design and first implementation slice.

## Release Readiness Snapshot

## Required Update Checklist (Every Significant Change)

1. Update relevant workstream row(s) in this board.
2. Add or refresh evidence link(s) (test command, workflow run, PR/commit).
3. Re-check release-readiness table if CI/workflows/runbooks changed.
4. Append one line in `Status Change Log`.

Suggested verification commands before marking a row as improved:

```bash
# Backend
cd backend && pytest -q

# Frontend
cd ../frontend && npm run lint && npm test -- --runInBand --watch=false

# CI workflow syntax (local sanity)
ruby -e 'require "yaml"; YAML.load_file(".github/workflows/ci.yml"); puts "ci.yml OK"'
```

| 2026-04-02 | Hardened the lexicon enrichment/import path against control-character corruption after a real `words.enriched.jsonl` snapshot import failure caused by embedded NUL bytes in translated strings. Enrichment normalization now rejects control characters at schema-validation time, JSONL writers fail fast before serializing rows that still contain them, and the compiled-review import path sanitizes control characters recursively before persistence as a defensive backstop for operator imports. | 2026-03-08 | Real selector-vs-rerank benchmark on tricky lemmas suggests the new grounded `rerank-senses` step is useful as a quality mode, but not a full replacement for deterministic ranking. On the 10-word batch (`right`, `direct`, `common`, `fine`, `fair`, `plain`, `check`, `charge`, `scale`, `break`), rerank changed all 10 selections and often removed obvious deterministic tails, but it also introduced some debatable substitutes, so the best near-term path is to keep improving deterministic ranking and use rerank selectively for high-polysemy review or premium-quality builds. | Codex | deterministic baseline via `./.venv-lexicon/bin/python -m tools.lexicon.cli build-base --max-senses 6 --output-dir /tmp/lexicon-rerank-benchmark-20260308 right direct common fine fair plain check charge scale break` (10 lexemes / 52 senses, pass), real rerank via `./.venv-lexicon/bin/python -m tools.lexicon.cli rerank-senses --snapshot-dir /tmp/lexicon-rerank-benchmark-20260308 --provider-mode openai_compatible_node --model gpt-5.4 --reasoning-effort low --candidate-limit 8 right direct common fine fair plain check charge scale break` (10 rerank rows, pass), compare via `./.venv-lexicon/bin/python -m tools.lexicon.cli compare-selection --snapshot-dir /tmp/lexicon-rerank-benchmark-20260308 --rerank-file /tmp/lexicon-rerank-benchmark-20260308/sense_reranks.jsonl --output /tmp/lexicon-rerank-benchmark-20260308/comparison.json` (`10/10` lexemes changed; clearer wins included removing `complain.v.01` from `plain`, dropping `check.n.09`, and replacing `break.v.40` / `break.n.11` tails). |

| 2026-03-28 | Improved `tools.lexicon.import_db` reliability and observability for large fixture loads, but not enough to make the full `9426`-row round-trip practical yet. The importer now commits in bounded chunks (`commit_every_rows`, default `250`) instead of holding the whole run in one giant transaction, and it skips several guaranteed-miss reads for brand-new rows (preloading existing words/phrases/references up front and avoiding existing meaning/example/translation/relation/run lookups when the parent row was just created).
